Thanks!

Specs :

Intel Celeron 2.60Ghz
1.5GB RAM
2 80GB HD - One Linux, One Windows
Matrox Parhelia 128MB

### Post by CrZy_T on 2007-10-21
I had some of the same problems. I had to reboot my computer every time I changed xorg.conf when using the mtx module. Simply restarting gdm gave me weird splash screen.

I fixed my xorg.conf and rebooted and now everything is working. Could you please paste your xorg.conf and mabye I'll be able to help.
